## Opcodes

```
  0: 0x1456 [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[26] = Entity->Race
  1: 0x145B [0x1A] CALL_SUBROUTINE(address=0x5CD6)
  2: 0x145E [0x66] LOAD_EXT_SCHEDULER_MAIN: Load scheduler "sha1" with entities [EventEntity, EventEntity], work=ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[27]
  3: 0x146D [0x53] WAIT_SCHEDULER_TASK: Wait for scheduler "sha1" with entities [EventEntity, EventEntity]
  4: 0x147A [0x00] END_REQSTACK()

  5: 0x5CD6 [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[27] = ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[26]
```
